margin-bottom:2px;  font-weight: 300;margin-top: 0px; font-family:'Noto Sans', sans-serif; letter-spacing: -0.2px; text-align:center;\");\n    untillDeadline.innerHTML=\"avant l’échéance\";\n  }\n\n\n  //\n\n\n\n  //\n\n\n  //add to stage\n  widget.appendChild(countDownBox)\n\n  countDownBox.appendChild(numbersBox);\n  countDownBox.appendChild(numbersDesc)\n\n  countDownBox.style.opacity=0;\n\n  countDownBox.appendChild(untillDeadline);\n  countDownBox.id=\"countDownBox\"\n\n\n\n}\n</script><style type=\"text/css\" media=\"all\" id=\"siteorigin-panels-grids-wp_head\">/* Layout 5615 */ #pg-5615-0 , #pg-5615-1 , #pg-5615-2 , #pg-5615-3 , #pg-5615-4 , #pg-5615-5 , #pg-5615-6 , #pl-5615 .panel-grid-cell .so-panel , #pl-5615 .panel-grid-cell .so-panel:last-child { margin-bottom:0px } #pg-5615-0 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-2 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-3 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-6 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-7 .panel-grid-cell { float:none } #pgc-5615-1-0 , #pgc-5615-1-1 , #pgc-5615-4-0 , #pgc-5615-4-1 , #pgc-5615-5-0 , #pgc-5615-5-1 { width:50% } #pg-5615-1 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-4 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-5 .panel-grid-cell { float:left } @media (max-width:767px){ #pg-5615-0 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-1 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-2 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-3 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-4 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-5 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-6 .panel-grid-cell , #pg-5615-7 .panel-grid-cell { float:none;width:auto } #pgc-5615-1-0 , #pgc-5615-4-0 , #pgc-5615-5-0 , #pl-5615 .panel-grid .panel-grid-cell-mobile-last { margin-bottom:0px } #pl-5615 .panel-grid , #pl-5615 .panel-grid-cell {  } #pl-5615 .panel-grid .panel-grid-cell-empty { display:none }  } </style>\t\t\n\t\t<style>\n\t\t\n\t\t.iw-so-acc-content {\n\t\t\tbackground:#FFF;\n\t\t}\n\n\n #pgc-195-2-0 a{\n\t border-top:1px solid #CCC;\n\tmargin-top:0;
